class Router extends HTMLElement {
    constructor() {
        super()
    }
    update() {
        Array.from(this.children).forEach(c=>{
            c.update()
        })
    }
    redirect(path) {
        window.history.pushState({}, '', path)
        this.update()
    }
}

class Route extends HTMLElement {
    constructor() {
      super();
    }
    connectedCallback() {
        this.path = this.getAttribute('path')
        this.to_render = this.hasAttribute('render') ? this.getAttribute('render') : this.innerHTML
        this.innerHTML = ''
    }
    update() {
        if (this.path === window.location.pathname) {
            this.innerHTML = this.to_render
        } else {
            this.innerHTML = ''
        }
    }
}
customElements.define('app-router', Router);
customElements.define('app-route', Route);

let sliders = [];

window.onresize = function(){
  const oldSliders = sliders.slice(0);
  sliders = [];
  oldSliders.forEach( slider => {
    initSlider(slider.element);
  });
};

function resolveSlider(element){
  return sliders.find( s => s.element === element || s.element.contains(element) );
}

function initSlider(element){
  const slideCount = element.getElementsByClassName("slide").length;
  const slider = {
    index: 1,
    autoChangeTime: 5000,
    timeoutFunction: null,
    element,
    length: slideCount,
    width: element.getBoundingClientRect().width * slideCount
  };
  element.querySelector(".slides").style.width = slider.width + "px";
  sliders.push(slider);
  moveSlide(element, 1);
}

// Next/previous controls
function moveSlide(element, n) {
  const slider = resolveSlider(element);
  showSlides(element, slider.index += n);
}

// Thumbnail image controls
function changeSlide(element, n) {
  const slider = resolveSlider(element);
  showSlides(element, slider.index = n);
}

function showSlides(element, n) {
  const slider = resolveSlider(element);
  const dots = slider.element.getElementsByClassName("dot");
  const slidesElement = slider.element.querySelector(".slides");
  
  if (n > slider.length) {slider.index = 1}
  if (n < 1) {slider.index = slider.length}
  
  slidesElement.style.left = `-${(slider.index - 1) * (slider.width / slider.length)}px`
  
  for (let i = 0; i < dots.length; i++) {
    dots[i].classList.remove("active");
  }
  dots[slider.index-1].classList.add("active");
  
  clearTimeout(slider.timeoutFunction);
  slider.timeoutFunction = setTimeout(() => {
    moveSlide(slider.element, 1);
  }, slider.autoChangeTime);
}

const EventEmitter = require('events')


class Queue extends EventEmitter {
    constructor() {
        super()
        this.items = []
        this.on('done', ()=>{
          this.items.shift()
          if(this.items[0]) this.items[0].exec()
        })
    }
    addItem(functionItem) {
        this.items.push({
            time: Date.now(),
            exec: () => functionItem().then(()=>this.emit('done'))
        })
        if(this.items.length === 1) {
          this.items[0].exec()
        }
    }
}
const q = new Queue()

q.addItem(async()=>console.log('bite'))

q.addItem(async()=>console.log('bite2'))

q.addItem(async()=>console.log('bite3'))

q.addItem(async()=>console.log('bite4'))

class Sessions {
  constructor(maxAge) {
    this.maxAge = maxAge;
    this.sessions = {};
    this.middleware.bind(this)
    this.genId.bind(this)
  }
  static genSecret(length) {
    const chars = "abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789/:;.?,%$*-+)(][}{#".split('')
    return new Array(length).fill(null).map(() => chars[Math.floor(Math.random() * chars.length)])
  }
  middleware(req, res, next) {
    if (!req.cookies.SESSID) res.cookie("SESSID", this.genId(), {
      maxAge: this.maxAge
    })
    if (!this.sessions[req.cookies.SESSID]) this.sessions[req.cookies.SESSID] = {}
    req.session = {
      get: (name) => this.sessions[req.cookies.SESSID][name],
      set: (name, value) => this.sessions[req.cookies.SESSID][name] = value,
      getRaw: () => this.sessions[req.cookies.SESSID],
      remove: () => {
        delete this.sessions[req.cookies.SESSID];
        res.cookie("SESSID", '', {
          expires: new Date(0)
        });
      }
    }
    next()
  }
  genId() {
    let current = Object.keys(this.sessions)[0]
    while (Object.keys(this.sessions).includes(current)) {
      current = Sessions.genSecret(150)
    }
    return current
  }
}

function sessionFactory(maxAge) {
  const session = new Sessions(maxAge);
  return session.middleware.bind(session);
}

Maintenant il connait son propre code
d'ailleurs qui l'a dit ?
const Ector = require('ector')
const Discord = require('discord.js')
const fs = require('fs').promises

const eddy = new Ector('Eddy')
const client = new Discord.Client({
    disableMentions: 'all'
})

const datasets = [
    "./reddit.json"
]

const allowedChannels = [
    '665906410881679360'
]
const disallowedChannels = [
    '622382371873882156',
    '622382349426098200',
    '622382324880900096'
]

function readIntents() {
    return fs.readFile('./intents.json').then(d=>JSON.parse(d).data)
}

function readDataset(dataset) {
    return fs.readFile(dataset).then(d=>JSON.parse(d).data)
}

async function addIntent(intent) {
    const intents = await readIntents()
    fs.writeFile('./intents.json', JSON.stringify({data: [...intents, intent]}, null, 2))
}

client.login(require('./token.json').token)

client.on('ready', async ()=>{
    console.log('=> Bot ready !')
    console.log('Loading intents...')
    const intents = await readIntents()
    intents.forEach(intent=>{
        eddy.addEntry(intent)
    })
    console.log('Intents loaded !')
    console.log('Loading datasets...')
    datasets.forEach(async dataset=>{
        console.log('Loading dataset '+dataset)
        const data = await readDataset(dataset)
        data.forEach(d=>{
            eddy.addEntry(d)
        })
        console.log('Dataset '+dataset+' loaded !')
    })
})

client.on('message', message=>{
    if(message.author.bot || message.system) return
    if(message.content.startsWith('\\')) return
    eddy.setUser(message.member.displayName)
    if(allowedChannels.includes(message.channel.id)) {
        eddy.addEntry(message.content)
        addIntent(message.content)
        return message.channel.send(eddy.generateResponse().sentence)
    }
    if(!disallowedChannels.includes(message.channel.id)) {
        addIntent(message.content)
        return eddy.addEntry(message.content)
    }
})
